A second line connects the airport train station and major attractions. For a sports loser like me, the only requirement for traveling is to have a subway. I only go to places that are accessible by subway.
Room facilities:
The executive room is okay and clean. Then there is a clean room, and the lounge is okay for dinner at night. It’s so cold at night in Shenyang that I don’t even want to go out.
Serve:
Basically everything is answered and can be delivered right away with just a phone call. swimming pool:
The pool is shallow and suitable for children to play. But the changing rooms and swimming pool are not clean.
breakfast:
The best thing is the chicken noodle soup, so you don’t have to go to Lao Four Seasons. Next is the tofu pudding, then the donuts and croissants are done well. Others are average.
Summary: The location is convenient, the food is okay, and the service is good. The hotel is not too new, there is no formaldehyde problem, and it is not too old to look bad. The price is more suitable for the whole family.

msg:The hotel is in a very good location, very close to the high-speed rail station. However, there are often traffic jams on Qingnian Street, so be careful to arrange your transportation time.
Facilities: Daily needs can be met, the rooms are all standard configuration, there are not too many thoughtful little settings ~
Hygiene: clean and tidy, no smell anywhere in the room, suitable experience
Environment: The room temperature is suitable for a Northeastern hotel. There are double-sided floor-to-ceiling windows with good lighting. The room space is large.
Service: The staff has a very good attitude, proactively inquires about needs, and gives some small fruits as a gift
important! important! Let’s talk about the shortcomings:
1. I ordered some personal items for takeout and came with a box of cut fruits, but the hotel does not have a robot to deliver it. I called the front desk and reported that it would not be delivered because of food safety management issues. I had to go to the bar to get it myself. As a hotel at this price, this should not be the case. .
2. The usual drinks and snacks in the indoor bar are normally given as free gifts without price tags and consumption tips. However, when checking out, I was told that there was a charge for consumption. Although they were waived in the end without payment, it was serious. It affects the customer's psychological experience. Charged items in the hotel should have consumption labels or consumption reminders. As a hotel owned by Hilton, we charge for a bottle of Coke, sparkling water, etc. There is no consumption notification, which is a bad review!
3. My friend came to pick me up. Without disturbing other vehicles, I only waited for 5 minutes for a parking space at the door before being chased away by security guards with a bad attitude.

posted:Posted August 21, 2021
msg:After a long time, I finally have time to write a review
The overall experience is average, but the price is cheap and the service attitude is okay
advantage:
1. The biggest advantage should be the service. We stayed in three rooms for two nights. One room had a broken air conditioner on the first day. As compensation, the front desk provided two breakfast buffets for the second day.
2. Convenient transportation, the subway station is next to the hotel, which makes it easy to travel
3. The price is very cheap, only six or seven hundred

Then talk about the shortcomings
1. The room landscape is outrageous, facing a large area of unfinished buildings, the so-called construction site landscape.
2. The room is extremely small
3. The facilities are inoperable, and the rubber ***** on the toilet door falls off, causing water to leak out
4. As a hotel in such a tall building, Hilton actually chose to arrange the guest rooms on the lower floors of the building. All other hotels I have stayed in are arranged on the top floor
5. The gym is not 24 hours a day. Go to the door at 11 o'clock in the evening and put a huge sign to write that it is closed. Although you can still enter by swiping your room card, the announcement is very uncomfortable. It is recommended to change it to unsupervised at night and use it independently. Will be much better
6. The bed linen is not clean, and the feet were bitten by bugs after taking a bath and going to bed
7. Check out the consultation and check-in experience, and give true feedback. The hotel said that it is impossible for it to have a sanitary problem, and will investigate it. Is it possible that emmmm I still wronged you, and then said that the next time I come to live will be upgraded, but there is a high probability that it will not be the next time. Would choose this one
8. As a 17-year-old guest who made a reservation with his own ID, paid and paid the deposit for three rooms, it was extremely difficult to check in early due to the delay of the family’s flight, saying that it did not comply with Hilton’s internal management system, and as far as I know At the age of sixteen and have economic income, it is in line with the full capacity to check in. I have not been able to check in at Marriott hotels in other cities before. Even if I gave the room card, I still said that I couldn't enter the system without face authentication.

In summary, in fact, the check-in experience is not satisfactory. Given the good service, give me a moderate review.

房間用不起Wi-Fi…在外邊就有，躺床上就沒了…？？？
一次性牙刷第一支拆出來還炸毛不能用…這？？

服務：客房服務餐食也太難吃了吧？？？直接沒吃完放房間門口了…presentation也很難評…保鮮膜上還沾着醬料…走點心？
餐廳的飯菜勉強能吃吧但是餐廳為啥不能備點濕巾？…工作人員找尋片刻答覆沒有…
電梯裏遇到一小哥，“禮貌招呼”後繼續45度斜靠外放刷**…我該誇他不專業但是有禮貌嗎？
都收了服務費了，能不能確保一下服務水準？
禮賓處餐廳個別工作人員態度還是可圈可點的…但總的來説非常失望，本來我是想退房時候跟前台投訴的……結果人家並不care我住得怎麼樣…我當時實在身體不舒服無力吐槽🙃

下次來瀋陽絕對不會再選擇這家希爾頓了…這次入住體驗讓我對希爾頓集團酒店的印象都變差了，之前住過的旗下酒店都還算滿意… 這家橫向對比真的比不了君悦朗廷🙂

酒店房間不錯，服務很好，能夠按照備註要求預留合適的房間。
房間內部寬敞，設施該有的都有，有小童浴巾、牙刷、沐浴液、洗髮水、拖鞋。

住店客人停車免費，地下三、四層可以隨便停，車位比較充足。
